< Review>
The premises are clean. An attendant is on duty. Debit/credit cards as well as coins are accepted. A coin changer is present. Opens at 7am; closes at ... 8pm??? Although several machines did not operate, the ones that did worked well. I didn't exactly time the wash machine, but it seemed to clean a load in 15-minutes. The washers range from small, $2.75 to 5-load-capacity at $7.75. and several sizes inbetween. Vending machines sell drinks and snacks. Pinball machines are there too. Except for the lunatic schizo woman who accused me of "rushing" her, calling me racist names, and telling me to get the f____ out of her face, it was a pleasurable experience.</Review>

First of all I have to give these guys kudos on the amazing remodel they did of this historic building. The details and craftsmanship is phenomenal.

I've eaten here now twice, and both times I left so happy and full. I had the blackened chicken sandwich the first time with sweet potatoe fries and it was one of the best samdwiches I've ever had.

The second time I ordered the blsck and blue flat bread and again was blown away by the quality of the steak, so juicy and tender. I've never had a flat bread I was crazy about till this one.

The staff here is so friendly and fast, I couldn't believe how quick my food came out, it was amazing.

The place wasn't packed, I was sat immediately and they had good music playing, I really love the decor of the restaurant, it totally fits the era.

Overall the place is very authentic and the history of the Sheepherders Inn going back to 1913. The staff showed me a bunch of the photos from when it was originally being built.

I highly reccomend this place, it's enjoyable and even affordable for the quality and portion of food you get. <review>I have been living here for a year and my experience has been great!

I relocated from LA and did not physically see my apartment until the day I moved. I only had seen pics and floorplans prior to renting. My must-haves were in-unit washer/dryer and they have it!

I am in the larger 1 bedroom floorplan (695 sq ft) with a wood burning fireplace.

One of the great things I love about my apartment is the massive bathroom. You can literally throw a party in it (lol). From the granite countertop to the spacious cabinets. While the shower/tub are on the other side of the bathroom. The washer/dryer is in a closet area completely tucked away.

My living room is also pretty spacious and can comfortably fit a sectional sofa. The wood burning fireplace is not only gorgeous but a lifesaver for the cold nights you'll often experience in the Bay Area. Which leads out to the covered balcony. I enjoy the fact that when it's raining outside you can still sit out there and not get soaking wet.

Overall, I am happy with my apartment and experience living at Artistry. Justin & Erica from the office team has always been super helpful. Anytime I have had an issue in my apartment the service team is very prompt on fixing it. The manager, Timicia is AMAZING, she is very responsive and keeps you in the loop on updates within the community, resident events, or just general questions!

I would renew here again!< /review>< pics>

<rating>1</rating>< text>
Train Horns. Do not live here if you are a light sleeper or cannot stand loud noise. I had moved here from the east coast a year ago, and wish I had read some of the reviews here beforehand.

The complex is located near 3 street crossings (65th, 66th, & 67th St), which trains are required by law to use their horn for each crossing at least once. This often lasts in 30 second intervals, at more than 20+ times a day. I typically would hear at least 3-5 trains every night between 9pm - 3am, which I was not able to sleep through for year.

If you are working from home during COVID, the train vibrations/horns will definitely interfere with meetings/calls. Spend some time at Public Market for a few hours to see if the location is the right fit for you.</text>

< Text>
I was relocating from New York and had been visiting apartments since the moment I stepped off the plane on Saturday morning. It was a frustrating couple of hours, as none of the apartments had the total package I was looking for. Artistry wasn't on my schedule for apartments to see, but I happened to pass it during my drive through Emeryville. Erica B was the leasing team member I was lucky to be paired with.

She made the experience very personal from the very beginning. She is similar in age and had similar interests, so we established rapport pretty quickly. She answered all of my questions very honestly, preparing me for what to expect throughout my stay. She even gave me tips on the type of cooling system I should get to keep my apartment at a comfortable temperature level.

I was originally looking for a 1br/1bath, with a pool being a must have amenity, however, because of the experience she created for me, I settled for a studio at Artistry. Artistry doesn't have a pool, but it does have a hot tub and a grilling area/court yard. Everything about it felt right instantly, which was definitely enough for me to be more flexible about what I was looking for.

Is there train noise? Yeah. Am I ok with it? Yeah.
Is there sometimes noise in the halls from other residents walking in or out? Yeah. I am also ok with it. I also see some comments about not getting all of the deposit back. The deposit for studios and 1 bedrooms are only $400... thats not much compared to most places in New York and some of the other places I visited in the Bay Area. Most of that deposit ends up going towards cleaning costs. Erica was very open about everything I should expect when I visited the apartment. Had she not told me, I would probably be much more irritated. She has been extremely transparent and helpful since I moved in on Tuesday and I feel extra comfortable knowing I can shoot her an email and get helped right away.

I have needed maintenance during the short time I've been here, for small things, such as, some tightening on some of the things in the apartment and help using the service elevator for furniture deliveries. Erica helped set that up immediately. Jorge came and fixed one of the cabinets in the bathroom. She asked also Jorge to meet my delivery guys the other morning. Jorge is also great! Super friendly and very helpful.

I'm a little unsure when I read the reviews below, as this has not been my experience with Artistry at all. It was exceptional.

Thanks again for the great service!< /Text>

<Resp>None</Resp><username>Jonathan Bowman<//username>< review>
Wow. Where do I start? This place has class, sophistication and more importantly brilliantly plated dishes that will have your mouth watering and your heart longing for more. First of all I'm not a fan of Chinese food but I am, however, a fan of Martin Yan. He's a brilliant entertainer, culinary master and an accomplished author. So naturally I was curious and when I took my family here I made sure to avoid anything Chinese. The odd thing is that his dishes are fusion based so it wasn't hard at all to avoid the traditional Chinese food you'd expect to see in a Chinese restaurant. I had some awesome chicken wings and satay to start. My kids had edamame and I ordered a small plate of calamari which was out of this world. Before I go any further I must say the prices were very reasonable and may even verge on cheap. Anyhow I decided that beef and broccoli sounded delish because of the fusion twist and sure enough it was! It tasted nothing like Chinese take-out. In fact it was brilliantly paired with some sort of curry-ginger sauce. WOW! Now for the best part! I finished the evening with a to-die-for fried banana ala mode. Now mind you I could have opted for plain old vanilla but I was feeling a bit wild so I went for the green tea ice cream! üçµ PHENOMENAL!!!!!!

So if you want a delicious and affordable place to taste amazing fusion dishes that verge on Thai-Indian and Chinese please go here! And don't forget the fried banana ala mode.</review>

<user_name>Chamar Moss</user_name><Date>1509192988318< /Date><rating>3< /rating><review>First, I say to the people complaining about having to pay back fees on their bills, take some responsibility. MID doesn't just shut off your power if you are late on 1 bill, it takes several, or a real high balance for them to terminate or shut off your service. I know because I had a rough time paying for a while due to losing a job. they do make you pay the full balance to get your service restored, but they also offer programs that can help reduce your bill and offer payment plans if you do not wait until it is too late to pay YOUR bill. They are a private company, not a public servant, they are in the business of making money. If you don't pay your bill, its the same as any place (car finance company) the bank that you have your mortgage through, if you don't pay your bill, you get evicted, you get repossessed etc etc... With that said, MID charges outrageous prices, their bills are confusing and always leave you thinking that they are overcharging you, the new "update for the website is NOT user friendly, and I do agree with what one customer said in that the service you receive depends on what kind of day the CSR you have contact with is having. As far as deposits go, I had to put down a $200 deposit like most people, but if you pay your bill on time for a full year, you will get the $200 deposit back in bill credits. I made my payments on time and in full, for a year and didn't have to pay my bill for 2 months and only had about half the bill to pay on the 3rd month. All said and done they are an average company. <date>1548295549331< /date><Text>Darkly wood panelled place, dine in the pseudo "old" style. Overstuffed stools, a couch or two and a secondary bar level stooped area make for abundant seating. Service was uneven, as it took the staff over 10 minutes to notice that we were there (not many of them were out) but once we were noticed, a number of servers and associated workers appeared, as if they were all occupied elsewhere and just got let out; it was odd. The service, once the servers were "out", was prompt and professional. Drinks are not cheap but I had the feeling they are trying to represent themselves as an "established" place but the feel was more if an "upscaley" place; we're popular and you're fortunate to be eating our fine food. The food was quite good. <Rating>5< /Rating><review>White Horse is a really great place to visit for delicious New Orleans Cajun. The food and drinks are very well priced for the outstanding quality you get, and the servers and bartenders are extremely knowledgeable as well. Feel safe when visiting, everything is being done with the COVID best practice requirements. Great happy hour offerings as well, especially for those that like 'Old Fashioneds'. I really liked and appreciated the old school music and old fashioned dim bar surroundings, it really was refreshing. The dark wood and red upholstery The exterior design is very tasteful and catches your attention when passing by. The set up works great for those looking for a group setting or even just for couples. I found the brunch menu to be especially enticing, I'm going to need to come back a couple of times to try out all the things that looked promising. The parking structure is right next door for maximum convenience. This place is truly a hidden gem amongst all the other great places in Pasadena. I'm also looking forward to checking out their sister location, Craft Hill, which I've heard great things about. Brandon was an amazing team member and recommended the fried chicken sandwich, which was fantastic. He knew all the items on the menu almost from memory and went above and beyond to walk me through everything. I'm glad I went with his recommendations. He also told me some cool things to do in the area and South Pasadena, so I have those on my list as well. They don't skip on the portions either, you'll definitely satisfy your appetite and probably have some leftovers as well. I can't think of much they can do to improve things, everything was so great! I plan on visiting again sooner rather than later.< /review>< Pictures>

< name>
James Wan</name>
<date>1583312770688</date><Rate>2</Rate>< Review>
A packed dining room and bar put this place quite in the limelight as you enter on a weekend evening. Unfortunately, there were far too many misses to honestly click on an extra star for the rating.

The bar seriously needs to pay attention to customers. Waiting for my party and waiting at the bar, and trying to get a drink was an impossible 5 minutes. They were treating me like I just came out of an AA meeting.

The menu seems to hit most of the notes for a hungry patron. At first glance, you can see it is well designed. Something for everyone wraps the context of each category. Fine Wagyu meats, a great burger, your standard salmon dish, and an attractive Southern Fried Chicken.

Dig deeper and you can find the pretentiousness of certain items. The use of Wagyu in smoked brisket, for example, is quite a redundancy. Why pay for a Wagyu priced cut that is supposed to be slow-smoked/cooked?

The Jumbalaya Rissoto is in fact not "risotto," and made with orzo pasta. Granted it is stated in the description as orzo, the title is completely misleading. If a person was gluten intolerant this would be a horrific experience. This dish is totally not worthy of the $26 price tag for a pasta dish.

The service felt like the servers were really working hard. I overheard a waiter mumbling about covering 8 large tables. I commend the service timing for everyone at the table.

The drinks here are very good. The bar certainly displays some craft behind their creations. I would return for their happy hour, and possibly a revisit for a sample of other items.

I do miss Cheval Blanc that once took this location to new heights in french cuisine.< /Review>

< review>
I've only come here for the bar and drinks, never had the food. The drinks are all great, well thought out, and delicious. They switch up the cocktail menu every couple of months, so there's always something new to try as well. For Pasadena, the drinks are fairly priced and the bartenders are super knowledgeable.

It can get pretty packed and hard to flag down someone to order a drink sometimes. It''s a great place to have some drinks before going to a club or just have a chill night talking with some friends.</review>

What a wonderful surprise!! The White Horse Lounge is a great place for family, out of town guest spot, romantic two or just friends! The food is an explosion of flavors and mouth watering treats! I kind you not.. the southern fried chicken is seasoned to delight, the Hoe cake made me moooan, the salmon avec haricot verts satisfies the palate with lightness.. and the drinks..well let's just say they don't hold back! The ambiance is Nu Oleans almost classic brothel style with elegant private cubbies tucked aside; it's warm and welcoming and smooth music playing in the background will catch you for a recognizable song.. the service is exceptional, making sure you're delighted to be there. The chef is to be applauded..my understanding is he's been there about a year and a half and he's for sure making a statement at the White Horse Lounge! Oh and did I mention the Blackberry peach cobbler!! The place is high on my list you won't be disappointed!!< /text>

<time>1548308477431<//time><rating>5< /rating>< text>
Update:
We stopped by and has Arroyo hamburger which was fantastic. Big Josh, the chef stopped by and revealed that the every ingrediants used here is from a local and certified grower. We had Judy taken care of us.

Josh was proud of his cooking style learned from her Japanese granma.

A classy place with great selection and service. We just dropped in and got hooked.

We sat in and Cesar took our order. He suggested Strawberry Buck and Peach Schnapps to start with which were both sweet drinks and fit the occasion. Bertta, the manager stopped by and chatted with us over the specials for the night.

The Bread and Butter we got was warmly toasted with some  greens and slice of pork. We ordered Porklion and Arroyo Burger. Both were good and tasty. The portions were adequate.

We ended with Pear cobbler with scoop of ice cream. Well made and filling.<//text>

<rate>4</rate>< Review>
We came to White Horse Lounge in Pasadena to celebrate a friend's birthday.
Love the beautiful bar area. It‚Äôs got that classic American bar vibe.
Since we have a large party, we were seated in the private room in the back.
Very simple one page menu. They have quite a few small bites that are great with drinks.

Market Hummus | $10
House Lavash, EVOO, Fresh Garnish
We ordered a few appetizers to share.
Market Hummus was just ok. It lacked flavor.

Seared Brussel Sprouts | $10
Smoked Tomatoes, Basil, Parmesan
Seared Brussel Sprouts was great. We enjoyed the addition of tomatoes and basil.

Garlic Truffle Fries | $9
Truffle Oil, Parmesan, Gremolata
We love the Garlic Truffle Fries. Thick and crunchy fries seasoned with truffle oil and cheese.

Bone-In New York 22 oz | $45
For steak orders, guests can pick 2 sides and a sauce for the meat.
A friend ordered the huge Bone-In New York, and she almost finished it!
She likes the steak, but didn‚Äôt like the cajun butter sauce.

Ribeye 16 oz | $35
Dr. P and I both ordered the Ribeye.
The steak was cooked perfectly. Very delicious.
For sides, I got the twice baked potato and corn succotash.
I enjoyed both. And the horseradish sauce was great with the steak.

The Black Sea | $25
Squid Ink Tagliolini, Dinapoli Tomato, Calamari, Prawn, Fin√©s Herbes
A few people ordered The Black Sea ‚Äì the squid ink seafood pasta.
Everyone said it was way too salty, and nobody liked it.

I like that we had the private room, and could be as loud as we want.
Service could be better. Our waitress didn‚Äôt check on us often.
We had to go out to find her a few times.
It was a really fun night with friends.</Review>
